<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сгустить.html>сгусти́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sgustítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сгущать.html>сгуща́ть</a></b>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сгущавший.html>сгуща́вший</a> (32152)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сгущавший.html>сгуща́вший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sguščávšij</span>)

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сгущать.html>сгуща́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sguščátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сгущаться.html>сгуща́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sguščátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сгуститься.html>сгусти́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to curdle, to clot, to thicken, to coagulate</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сгущать.html>сгуща́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sguščátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***сдавать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сдавать.html>сдава́ть</a> (3451)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сдать.html>сдать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sdatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ва́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-vátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сдавать.html>сдава́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sdavátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сдать.html>сдать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to deliver, to hand in, to hand over</li>
<li>to return, to turn in
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:сдавать.html>сдава́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:вещь.html>ве́щи</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:багаж.html>бага́ж</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>sdavátʹ</b> véšči v bagáž</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to check/register one's luggage</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:сдавать.html>сдава́ть</a></strong> <a href = vnd.unilang:дело.html>дела́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">sdavátʹ delá</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to turn over one's duties</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:сдавать.html>сдава́ть</a></b> внаём</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>sdavátʹ</b> vnajóm</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to let, to let out, to hire out</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:сдавать.html>сдава́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:аренда.html>аре́нду</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>sdavátʹ</b> v aréndu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to lease, to grant on lease, to rent</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><i>(a fortress, city etc.)</i> to surrender, to yield</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">card games</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to deal</li>
<li>to take/pass <i>(an exam)</i></li>
<li>to be weakened, to be in a reduced state</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сдавать.html>сдава́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sdavátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сдаваться.html>сдава́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sdavátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сдаться.html>сда́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to surrender, to yield</li>
<li>to give up, to give in</li>
<li>to give in, to give way</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сдавать.html>сдава́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sdavátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> impersonal<span class="ib-comma">,</span> imperfective only</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to seem
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:казаться.html>каза́ться</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">kazátʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сдавить.html>сдави́ть</a> (12904)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">с-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">s-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:давить.html>дави́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">davítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сдавить.html>сдави́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sdavítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сдавливать.html>сда́вливать</a></b>)

***сдать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сдать.html>сдать</a> (2002)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">с-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">s-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дать.html>дать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">datʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сдать.html>сдать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sdatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сдавать.html>сдава́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to deliver, to hand in, to hand over
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:учитель.html>учи́тель</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сказать.html>сказа́л</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:сдать.html>сдать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:сочинение.html>сочине́ния</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Učítelʹ skazál <b>sdatʹ</b> sočinénija.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">The teacher told us to turn in our compositions .</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to return, to turn in
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:сдать.html>сдать</a></strong> <a href = vnd.unilang:вещь.html>ве́щи</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:багаж.html>бага́ж</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">sdatʹ véšči v bagáž</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to check/register one's luggage</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:сдать.html>сдать</a></strong> <a href = vnd.unilang:дело.html>дела</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">sdatʹ dela</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to turn over one's duties</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сдать.html>сдать</a> внаем</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">sdatʹ vnajem</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to let, to let out, to hire out</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сдать.html>сдать</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:аренда.html>аре́нду</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">sdatʹ v aréndu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to lease (out), to grant on lease (out), to rent (out)</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive or intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to surrender, to yield
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:противник.html>проти́вник</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:сдать.html>сда́л</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:город.html>го́род</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:без.html>без</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:бой.html>бо́я</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Protívnik <b>sdal</b> górod bez bója.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">The enemy surrendered the town without a fight.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive or intransitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> card games</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to deal</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive or intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to take/pass, to usually about an exam
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жало.html>пе́тька</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:сдать.html>сда́л</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:экзамен.html>экза́мен</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:без.html>без</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:особый.html>осо́бых</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:усилие.html>уси́лий</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Pétʹka <b>sdal</b> ekzámen bez osóbyx usílij.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Peter passed the exam without much effort.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to be weakened, to be in a reduced state
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:твой.html>Твой</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:отец.html>оте́ц</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совсем.html>совсе́м</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:сдать.html>сда́л</a></b>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Tvoj otéc sovsém <b>sdal</b>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Your father's health declined a lot.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to move back a bit (like while driving)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чтобы.html>что́бы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:повернуть.html>поверну́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:нужный.html>ну́жно</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>бы́ло</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сначала.html>снача́ла</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:сдать.html>сдать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:назад.html>наза́д</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Štóby povernútʹ núžno býlo snačála <b>sdatʹ</b> nazád.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">In order to turn he first had to <i>move backwards a bit</i>.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сдача.html>сда́ча</a> (5438)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сдача.html>сда́ча</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sdáča</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сдача.html>сда́чи</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сдача.html>сда́чи</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сдача.html>сда́ч</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>delivery</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">by extension</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> fighting back, hitting back the offender</li>
<li>surrender</li>
<li>change <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">money given back when a customer hands over more than the exact price of an item</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>deal (card game)</li>
<li>letting out, leasing out <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">property; usually followed by <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">внаём</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vnajóm</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сдвинуть.html>сдви́нуть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sdvínutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="None mention" lang="ru">-∅</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-∅</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span><sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сдвиг.html>сдвиг</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sdvig</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сдвиг.html>сдви́га</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сдвиг.html>сдви́ги</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сдвиг.html>сдви́гов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>shift, displacement
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сдвиг.html>сдвиг</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:фаза.html>фа́зе</a> <i>(idiom)</i></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">sdvig po fáze <i>(idiom)</i></i> ― <span class="e-translation">light insanity</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:сдвиг.html>сдвиг</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:фаза.html>фа́з</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>sdvig</b> faz</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">phase shift/displacement; lag</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>change for the better, progress, improvement</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">geology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> displacement, dislocation</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">engineering</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> shear</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сдвигаться.html>сдвига́ться</a> (23906)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сдвигать.html>сдвига́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sdvigátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сдвигаться.html>сдвига́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sdvigátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сдвинуться.html>сдви́нуться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to move, to budge</li>
<li>to come/draw together</li>
<li>to move forward, to get going, to improve</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сдвигать.html>сдвига́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sdvigátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
